				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Ach Gott, wie manches Herzeleid, BWV 3 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1725 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Religious_works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Religious works</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="28 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_4_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 4 voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>

<th class="wi_head">Work Title

<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Ach Gott, wie manches Herzeleid

</th>
<td>BWV 3&#160;; BC A 33
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 4
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>A major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements:
<ol><li>Chorus: Ach Gott, wie manches Herzeleid
</li><li>Recitativo (tenor, soprano, alto, bass): Wie schwerlich lässt sich Fleisch und Blut
</li><li>Aria (bass): Empfind ich Höllenangst und Pein
</li><li>Recitativo (tenor): Es mag mir Leib und Geist verschmachten
</li><li>Duet Aria (soprano, alto): Wenn Sorgen auf mich dringen
</li><li>Chorale: Erhalt mein Herz im Glauben rein
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>

</td></tr>
